            <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                      id="H70A234DB1BF94EAF94978E90C4584C32"
                      qb-display-quote="yes"
                      section-type="subsequent-section">
               105.
               INTERNATIONAL MECHANISM TO USE RUSSIAN SOVEREIGN ASSETS AND RUSSIAN AGGRESSOR STATE SOVEREIGN ASSETS TO PROVIDE FOR THE RECONSTRUCTION OF UKRAINE
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H66BCF0E9D1FC4FFDB02439AD6C2CE1F6"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (a)
                  In general
                  The President shall take such actions as the President determines appropriate to coordinate with the G7, the European Union, Australia, and other partners and allies of the United States regarding the disposition of immobilized Russian aggressor state sovereign assets, including seeking to establish an international mechanism with foreign partners, including Ukraine, the G7, the European Union, Australia, and other partners and allies of the United States, for the purpose of assisting Ukraine, which may include the establishment of an international fund to be known as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">Ukraine Compensation Fund, that may receive and use assets in the Ukraine Support Fund established under section 104(c) and contributions from foreign partners that have also frozen or seized Russian aggressor state sovereign assets to assist Ukraine, including byâ€”
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H78A825C0203F43209366E422BB57D381"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (1)
                     supporting a register of damage to serve as a record of evidence and for assessment of the financially assessable damages to Ukraine resulting from the invasions of Ukraine by the Russian Federation and operations or actions in support thereof;
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HC960C1F9995C405299C3388A70277795"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (2)
                     establishing a mechanism to compensate Ukraine for damages caused by Russiaâ€™s internationally wrongful acts connected with the invasions of Ukraine;
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HB5ECE83801ED4FEB9DA1220BC21B6B60"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (3)
                     ensuring distribution of those assets or the proceeds of those assets based on determinations under that mechanism; and
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H919178C89C7849E4992298A87308E88F"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (4)
                     taking such other actions as may be necessary to carry out this section.
                  
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H363FB384FCCC4CE2900ABC0DBFAE43B5"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (b)
                  Authorization for deposit in the Ukraine Compensation Fund
                  Upon the President reaching an agreement or arrangement to establish a common international mechanism pursuant to subsection (a) or at any time thereafter, the Secretary of State may, pursuant to the authority conferred by and subject to the limitations described in section 104(f) and subject to the limitations described in subsection (e), transfer funds from the Ukraine Support Fund established under section 104(d) to a fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a).
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H5D7BFE98BF4E447EB110ABDDFDBFE235"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (c)
                  Notification
                  The President shall notify the appropriate congressional committees not later than 30 days after entering into any new bilateral or multilateral agreement or arrangement under subsection (a).
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="HC711994E03574FF2B34FABAB0AB809A6"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (d)
                  Good governance
                  The Secretary of State, in consultation with the Secretary of the Treasury, shallâ€”
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H4CD4A4C0F778455CA0078F399F675290"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (1)
                     seek to ensure that any fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) operates in accordance with established international accounting principles;
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H4E6E4F3DF32247D09C4DE5DA1FF9B6D7"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (2)
                     seek to ensure that any fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) isâ€”
                     <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="H09A829E87AC24C628A759EB193E744B9"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (A)
                        staffed, operated, and administered in accordance with established accounting rules and governance procedures, including providing for payment of reasonable expenses from the fund for the governance and operation of the fund and the tribunal;
                     
                     <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HB378F487A5C24DB5A06AC455522BC8CE"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (B)
                        operated transparently as to all funds transfers, filings, and decisions; and
                     
                     <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HB7977CF808E542B5BDBF8F7C47FB2181"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (C)
                        audited on a regular basis by an independent auditor, in accordance with internationally accepted accounting and auditing standards;
                     
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H71D19AB20D394BFE96F3E164516853F8"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (3)
                     seek to ensure that any audits of any fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) shall be made available to the public; and
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H245F3CDE032A4E158B2F4E988DFDE4AE"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (4)
                     ensure that any audits of any fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) shall be reviewed and reported on by the Government Accountability Office to the appropriate congressional committees and the public.
                  
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H0B054A2185DA44F4876FF1DBBDF25467"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (e)
                  Limitation on transfer of funds
                  No funds may be transferred from the Ukraine Support Fund to a fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) unless the President certifies to the appropriate congressional committees thatâ€”
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H00DB1632172E403C9702FEBAE6A188DA"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (1)
                     the institution housing the fund or mechanism has a plan to ensure transparency and accountability for all funds transferred to and from the fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a); and
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H7BB695B552A64B6ABFE35970DFB65A28"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (2)
                     the President has transmitted the plan required under paragraph (1) to the appropriate congressional committees in writing.
                  
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H256AB529597A445BB53661B30170C3AE"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (f)
                  Joint resolution of disapproval
                  No funds may be transferred from the Ukraine Support Fund to a fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a) if, within 30 days of receipt of the notification required under subsection (c)(2), a joint resolution is enacted prohibiting the transfer.
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="HBAFCC81D5331426E8A38D09B97B34FB0"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (g)
                  Report
                  Not later than 90 days after the date of the enactment of this division, and not less frequently than every 90 days thereafter, the President shall submit to the appropriate congressional committees a report that includes the following:
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HE76BA8C3E2044819ABD935F585492085"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (1)
                     An accounting of funds in any fund or mechanism established consistent with subsection (a).
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H862FA19CAE274AA3903BA37CC0EC14E7"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (2)
                     Any information regarding the disposition of any such fund or mechanism that has been transmitted to the President by the institution housing the fund or mechanism during the period covered by the report.
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H74F4C899FFAD42D1AF6DED7031AC0E15"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (3)
                     A description of United States multilateral and bilateral diplomatic engagement with allies and partners of the United States that also have immobilized Russian sovereign assets to allow for compensation for Ukraine during the period covered by the report.
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H3AF03B7F0361440CA408D4D0F39C00AC"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (4)
                     An outline of steps taken to carry out this section during the period covered by the report.
                  
               
            
            <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                      id="H0A90885595C44D518972E2907DA815E3"
                      qb-display-quote="yes"
                      section-type="subsequent-section">
               106.
               REPORT ON USE OF TRANSFERRED RUSSIAN SOVEREIGN ASSETS FOR RECONSTRUCTION
               Not later than 90 days after the date of the enactment of this division, and every 180 days thereafter, the Secretary of State, in consultation with the Secretary of the Treasury, shall submit to the appropriate congressional committees a report that containsâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H593FBEFCEFCD4E43BBB0174299BE94F3"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  the amount and source of Russian sovereign assets seized, transferred, or confiscated pursuant to section 104(b);
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H67CDDEEF61FE4287A56A048AF85A5184"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  the amount and source of funds deposited into the Ukraine Support Fund under section 104(b)(3); and
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HAD406E3520D94C4CB971B87F2F5DD5BF"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  a detailed description and accounting of how such funds were used to meet the purposes described in section 104(f). 
               
            
            <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                      id="HBDBD000E32CD4CC59E62CFD2184F1454"
                      qb-display-quote="yes"
                      section-type="subsequent-section">
               107.
               ASSESSMENT BY SECRETARY OF STATE AND ADMINISTRATOR OF USAID ON RECONSTRUCTION AND REBUILDING NEEDS OF UKRAINE
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="H6AA2EB3808F14A8E9D80BF91399EE9B8"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (a)
                  In general
                  Not later than 180 days after the date of the enactment of this division, the Secretary of State, in consultation with the Administrator of the United States Agency for International Development, shall submit to the appropriate congressional committees an assessment of the most pressing needs of Ukraine for reconstruction, rebuilding, and humanitarian aid.
               
               <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                            id="HC763D672D52D4C6898F11A49C0A1C0C5"
                            qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (b)
                  Elements
                  The assessment required by subsection (a) shall include the following:
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HA2F0677225414D58B4D2B24A16301148"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (1)
                     An estimate of the rebuilding and reconstruction needs of Ukraine, as of the date of the assessment, resulting from the unlawful invasion of Ukraine by the Russian Federation, includingâ€”
                     <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="H24EFEA6A314644BCBD92492F7B0E6576"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (A)
                        a description of the sources and methods for the estimate; and
                     
                     <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HCFB73AA6ABC44AD3A3A4157E494C8461"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (B)
                        an identification of the locations or regions in Ukraine with the most pressing needs.
                     
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HA0EF175BC6814B44B73C26E390B53D36"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (2)
                     An estimate of the humanitarian needs, as of the date of the assessment, of the people of Ukraine, including Ukrainians residing inside the internationally recognized borders of Ukraine or outside those borders, resulting from the unlawful invasion of Ukraine by the Russian Federation.
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H8288A2FF69B74B388792F1C96FA20BDF"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (3)
                     An assessment of the extent to which the needs described in paragraphs (1) and (2) have been met or funded, by any source, as of the date of the assessment.
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H068FBFB633224E5BA1BA740AEFEE1BE2"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (4)
                     A plan to engage in robust multilateral and bilateral diplomacy to ensure that allies and partners of the United States, particularly in the European Union as Ukraine seeks accession to the European Union, increase their commitment to Ukraineâ€™s reconstruction.
                  
                  <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H30EFEC941B70400C8D674A045C0F6962"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (5)
                     An identification of which such needs should be prioritized, including any assessment or request by the Government of Ukraine with respect to the prioritization of such needs.
                  
               
            
            <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                      id="H331F0E1EECBB4D8EBF526996D55FDDBB"

         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"

            2.
            INCLUSION OF INFORMATION ON EMERGING TECHNOLOGICAL DEVELOPMENTS IN ANNUAL CHINA MILITARY POWER REPORT

                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general

               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"

                           qb-display-quote="yes">

                  The implications for the national security of the United States as a result of the leadership or dominance by the Peopleâ€™s Republic of China in each such identified field and associated supply chains.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"

                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC7C65C152A124E7581A2BE87D8F6F463"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">

         H
         Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="HAB71148D0F3D490CAADB3AD0AF49921C"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            1.
            SHORT TITLE
            This division may be cited as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">
                  Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act
               .
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="HB72D71B2E6EA4286949A14E8B4253224"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            2.
            PROHIBITION OF FOREIGN ADVERSARY CONTROLLED APPLICATIONS
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H052BF57E9C8746E7A1B93A2B38E1396A"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H58B63000DC234D6F8EF4477EFE07D700"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Prohibition of foreign adversary controlled applications
                  It shall be unlawful for an entity to distribute, maintain, or update (or enable the distribution, maintenance, or updating of) a foreign adversary controlled application by carrying out, within the land or maritime borders of the United States, any of the following:
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC812013EFF46487F958F2ACA797181E0"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     Providing services to distribute, maintain, or update such foreign adversary controlled application (including any source code of such application) by means of a marketplace (including an online mobile application store) through which users within the land or maritime borders of the United States may access, maintain, or update such application.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H9574CC1E76A845E08021EACA09E0BE1E"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Providing internet hosting services to enable the distribution, maintenance, or updating of such foreign adversary controlled application for users within the land or maritime borders of the United States.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H5E38C02E012E4FB5A5CCF1573A786032"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Applicability
                  Subject to paragraph (3), this subsection shall applyâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H636689BA78CF41E1BCDBDC65506A015B"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     in the case of an application that satisfies the definition of a foreign adversary controlled application pursuant to subsection (g)(3)(A), beginning on the date that is 270 days after the date of the enactment of this division; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H24E3290075414FC08C3855C9FD84A471"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     in the case of an application that satisfies the definition of a foreign adversary controlled application pursuant to subsection (g)(3)(B), beginning on the date that is 270 days after the date of the relevant determination of the President under such subsection.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H22D8E2C85C144E68BDA42909FF197DB3"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  Extension
                  With respect to a foreign adversary controlled application, the President may grant a 1-time extension of not more than 90 days with respect to the date on which this subsection would otherwise apply to such application pursuant to paragraph (2), if the President certifies to Congress thatâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC88194A64F774FE4BEF0658100F7E703"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     a path to executing a qualified divestiture has been identified with respect to such application;
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H08E969FBC3354689872A544F1FD3C70C"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     evidence of significant progress toward executing such qualified divestiture has been produced with respect to such application; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HB202C1A5F2EB44ADA61FBDD2F6B2480B"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     there are in place the relevant binding legal agreements to enable execution of such qualified divestiture during the period of such extension.
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H9031D21879F14124B906F1DDCE9BD2E3"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Data and information portability to alternative applications
               Before the date on which a prohibition under subsection (a) applies to a foreign adversary controlled application, the entity that owns or controls such application shall provide, upon request by a user of such application within the land or maritime borders of United States, to such user all the available data related to the account of such user with respect to such application. Such data shall be provided in a machine readable format and shall include any data maintained by such application with respect to the account of such user, including content (including posts, photos, and videos) and all other account information.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HA57EDFC53CF14F2F90DF12402517E1F2"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Exemptions
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HEF955C76B75547BB8D89B56C997B3CE9"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Exemptions for qualified divestitures
                  Subsection (a)â€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H1053D7BA6C604B7FB4CAA89E8385DB31"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     does not apply to a foreign adversary controlled application with respect to which a qualified divestiture is executed before the date on which a prohibition under subsection (a) would begin to apply to such application; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HE8F307B868A34DC4A93BBE404CEA2FA8"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     shall cease to apply in the case of a foreign adversary controlled application with respect to which a qualified divestiture is executed after the date on which a prohibition under subsection (a) applies to such application.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HC9FE2AF6E8D8429C80F26D907F2AC379"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Exemptions for certain necessary services
                  Subsections (a) and (b) do not apply to services provided with respect to a foreign adversary controlled application that are necessary for an entity to attain compliance with such subsections.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H442D431CB5134108A7CF27D876EBF1BD"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               Enforcement
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA5C1034A0F114069AEC9973236865CED"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Civil penalties
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H419825B6A4CD428F95F74D9B82FC39B1"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     Foreign adversary controlled application violations
                     An entity that violates subsection (a) shall be subject to pay a civil penalty in an amount not to exceed the amount that results from multiplying $5,000 by the number of users within the land or maritime borders of the United States determined to have accessed, maintained, or updated a foreign adversary controlled application as a result of such violation.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H9C454A542ED14F3A9D856C1019D16754"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Data and information violations
                     An entity that violates subsection (b) shall be subject to pay a civil penalty in an amount not to exceed the amount that results from multiplying $500 by the number of users within the land or maritime borders of the United States affected by such violation.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H8A9E26E29D974E6E9CAA7F623AEB7049"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Actions by Attorney General
                  The Attorney Generalâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H494E6796D1A2400FAD81F5331B7E39DB"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     shall conduct investigations related to potential violations of subsection (a) or (b), and, if such an investigation results in a determination that a violation has occurred, the Attorney General shall pursue enforcement under paragraph (1); and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H11D0CB093789416EB5E0D7ECA46AEFEF"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     may bring an action in an appropriate district court of the United States for appropriate relief, including civil penalties under paragraph (1) or declaratory and injunctive relief.
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HE04006E91C424E9C8902B7C91C26EA42"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (e)
               Severability
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HDA068CFB9B044F64AA9EE6E863AA0670"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  If any provision of this section or the application of this section to any person or circumstance is held invalid, the invalidity shall not affect the other provisions or applications of this section that can be given effect without the invalid provision or application.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H0EC262B8CA8A471B996F2FEE4E37886C"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Subsequent determinations
                  If the application of any provision of this section is held invalid with respect to a foreign adversary controlled application that satisfies the definition of such term pursuant to subsection (g)(3)(A), such invalidity shall not affect or preclude the application of the same provision of this section to such foreign adversary controlled application by means of a subsequent determination pursuant to subsection (g)(3)(B).
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H18CC8E7783F54FCB9DB00870A18C8CBD"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (f)
               Rule of construction
               Nothing in this division may be construedâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HC9DDAFD483E445058F1FE2BA4601F183"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  to authorize the Attorney General to pursue enforcement, under this section, other than enforcement of subsection (a) or (b);
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H79909BB2BC104EF2BC466C3CE1930AF6"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  to authorize the Attorney General to pursue enforcement, under this section, against an individual user of a foreign adversary controlled application; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H2AAD2F586DD94089A3B7D4BE1E3BE30F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  except as expressly provided herein, to alter or affect any other authority provided by or established under another provision of Federal law.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H2D71AF0F43634217B24D42592CA6CF6F"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (g)
               Definitions
               In this section:
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HCFF3EA48E81E46A38148C5312CE80E8A"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Controlled by a foreign adversary
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">controlled by a foreign adversary means, with respect to a covered company or other entity, that such company or other entity isâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H9C3A5E9F5C8B4553897F248B068F1232"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     a foreign person that is domiciled in, is headquartered in, has its principal place of business in, or is organized under the laws of a foreign adversary country;
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H33C1F02440CA492ABFEDEC8DB495DAF6"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     an entity with respect to which a foreign person or combination of foreign persons described in subparagraph (A) directly or indirectly own at least a 20 percent stake; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H852F10ACD16B4CC98549BE66332FB7D6"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     a person subject to the direction or control of a foreign person or entity described in subparagraph (A) or (B).
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H046152EA805B4BB59EF4B0D61FC28955"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Covered company
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H144427AF18354C6B82642C20D77043BD"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     In general
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">covered company means an entity that operates, directly or indirectly (including through a parent company, subsidiary, or affiliate), a website, desktop application, mobile application, or augmented or immersive technology application thatâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H21694C7B35D74736901137CF4C0870D1"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        permits a user to create an account or profile to generate, share, and view text, images, videos, real-time communications, or similar content;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HE9A287BADE704149A56CE757C6333722"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        has more than 1,000,000 monthly active users with respect to at least 2 of the 3 months preceding the date on which a relevant determination of the President is made pursuant to paragraph (3)(B); 
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H20449E048F9F46999ACE330FF40F142A"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iii)
                        enables 1 or more users to generate or distribute content that can be viewed by other users of the website, desktop application, mobile application, or augmented or immersive technology application; and
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HA732E2B22473449B87D3CA01317B39DB"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iv)
                        enables 1 or more users to view content generated by other users of the website, desktop application, mobile application, or augmented or immersive technology application.
                     
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H1CC4FCDAE2F54BA1BC38BBA071BC5050"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Exclusion
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">covered company does not include an entity that operates a website, desktop application, mobile application, or augmented or immersive technology application whose primary purpose is to allow users to post product reviews, business reviews, or travel information and reviews.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H0A2584ACDBA6421CB9228F949380BDFB"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  Foreign adversary controlled application
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">foreign adversary controlled application means a website, desktop application, mobile application, or augmented or immersive technology application that is operated, directly or indirectly (including through a parent company, subsidiary, or affiliate), byâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HFC88714526AB4B2483411D1E7B1AD372"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     any ofâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H35C37989583D4F38B8484CC8478DAA65"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        ByteDance, Ltd.;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H5449DE1453A54E7889D2B9D6131379B9"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        TikTok;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HA68DA7D1C4F04F91B45DEBFB2CF5A4BA"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iii)
                         a subsidiary of or a successor to an entity identified in clause (i) or (ii) that is controlled by a foreign adversary; or
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H978B51D28C444AA3AA9A44E8D54689DE"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iv)
                        an entity owned or controlled, directly or indirectly, by an entity identified in clause (i), (ii), or (iii); or
                     
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H1091548C462F4DABA787D2F6B52406EC"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     a covered company thatâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H819F8730A970403CA6D8F38185089094"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        is controlled by a foreign adversary; and
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HC983D075793644D698D2342BEA2D707D"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        that is determined by the President to present a significant threat to the national security of the United States following the issuance ofâ€”
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HD0FE3F1276494BBB8D41ED002D521C05"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (I)
                           a public notice proposing such determination; and
                        
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HA87C0E697E1246779388E64CC8D4A12A"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (II)
                           a public report to Congress, submitted not less than 30 days before such determination, describing the specific national security concern involved and containing a classified annex and a description of what assets would need to be divested to execute a qualified divestiture.
                        
                     
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H14ADA5ED58F64079B9A80EF8768B536B"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (4)
                  Foreign adversary country
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">foreign adversary country means a country specified in section 4872(d)(2) of title 10, United States Code.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HBEA9402036D147F8895B7617B0680E10"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (5)
                  Internet hosting service
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">internet hosting service means a service through which storage and computing resources are provided to an individual or organization for the accommodation and maintenance of 1 or more websites or online services, and which may include file hosting, domain name server hosting, cloud hosting, and virtual private server hosting.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H57DED9B1744D4B8AB0ED5B3A611E0469"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (6)
                  Qualified divestiture
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">qualified divestiture means a divestiture or similar transaction thatâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC7FAA3514FD94BD88849A370AB4E4EF8"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     the President determines, through an interagency process, would result in the relevant foreign adversary controlled application no longer being controlled by a foreign adversary; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HEDC02B8DE8754ABC97BC9710C50427BE"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     the President determines, through an interagency process, precludes the establishment or maintenance of any operational relationship between the United States operations of the relevant foreign adversary controlled application and any formerly affiliated entities that are controlled by a foreign adversary, including any cooperation with respect to the operation of a content recommendation algorithm or an agreement with respect to data sharing.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD6A1DF7D951C4C9792CC26B8CB3C7E85"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (7)
                  Source code
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">source code means the combination of text and other characters comprising the content, both viewable and nonviewable, of a software application, including any publishing language, programming language, protocol, or functional content, as well as any successor languages or protocols.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HC09ED8B4F91A4D71A0B2A54CBA98F76F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (8)
                  United states
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">United States includes the territories of the United States.
               
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H064C385070114C3A8DA14F68F7405CB0"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            3.
            JUDICIAL REVIEW
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H9BBA895414034474899692215D769195"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               Right of action
               A petition for review challenging this division or any action, finding, or determination under this division may be filed only in the United States Court of Appeals for the District of Columbia Circuit.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HAA1F28EFA7854EC0BD1DADB0F0358BD5"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Exclusive jurisdiction
               The United States Court of Appeals for the District of Columbia Circuit shall have exclusive jurisdiction over any challenge to this division or any action, finding, or determination under this division.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H19E16F7F5C4941BC90E945791204E881"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Statute of limitations
               A challenge may only be broughtâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD9DE0676B0A841C98E76C54C1031ABC0"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  in the case of a challenge to this division, not later than 165 days after the date of the enactment of this division; and
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H98C024B0AC6B453B915C47821338C31D"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  in the case of a challenge to any action, finding, or determination under this division, not later than 90 days after the date of such action, finding, or determination.
               
            
         
      
      
         I
         Protecting Americansâ€™ Data from Foreign Adversaries Act of 2024
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="HB57C7BBE304640C5AED4B30B59291365"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            1.
            SHORT TITLE
            This division may be cited as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">
                  Protecting Americansâ€™ Data from Foreign Adversaries Act of 2024
               .
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H8A6F028CF82F488A974B9159A0CFBE01"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            2.
            PROHIBITION ON TRANSFER OF PERSONALLY IDENTIFIABLE SENSITIVE DATA OF UNITED STATES INDIVIDUALS TO FOREIGN ADVERSARIES
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H54314678A0A941969EDCB535596ADED2"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               Prohibition
               It shall be unlawful for a data broker to sell, license, rent, trade, transfer, release, disclose, provide access to, or otherwise make available personally identifiable sensitive data of a United States individual toâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD474BAF2D28642BCA6E93E4C2FAD83E4"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  any foreign adversary country; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HE7930600F74F4F9D82107A1C78195A3D"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  any entity that is controlled by a foreign adversary.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HB35778E918C54B44A6E852F2B3D0FF6D"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Enforcement by Federal Trade Commission
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H5B5A49693DB948E095E6AFDE349A8432"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Unfair or deceptive acts or practices
                  A violation of this section shall be treated as a violation of a rule defining an unfair or a deceptive act or practice under section 18(a)(1)(B) of the Federal Trade Commission Act (15 U.S.C. 57a(a)(1)(B)).
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HEC57A04DF1AE4A7D9EF7503D9D205109"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Powers of Commission
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HECB3E709A20C4E259F96D7957D8F6E71"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     In general
                     The Commission shall enforce this section in the same manner, by the same means, and with the same jurisdiction, powers, and duties as though all applicable terms and provisions of the Federal Trade Commission Act (15 U.S.C. 41 et seq.) were incorporated into and made a part of this section.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HF99BB1BA2E3C4B578B7C0295F4258EE1"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Privileges and immunities
                     Any person who violates this section shall be subject to the penalties and entitled to the privileges and immunities provided in the Federal Trade Commission Act.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD4BAEB608EBA440C8408558EFAC80B8F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  Authority preserved
                  Nothing in this section may be construed to limit the authority of the Commission under any other provision of law.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HD9B51348ADFB44E8AD4F2B7BEEB77645"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Definitions
               In this section:
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H84B2B34D4FDB46BF977659A00CD23FB7"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Commission
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">Commission means the Federal Trade Commission. 
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H2F69E2439A0E45F4B99540A058EAE88E"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Controlled by a foreign adversary
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">controlled by a foreign adversary means, with respect to an individual or entity, that such individual or entity isâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H81C64CA94D5E41499F21747E208C3FB1"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     a foreign person that is domiciled in, is headquartered in, has its principal place of business in, or is organized under the laws of a foreign adversary country;
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HE2EED6ABEA4A4F7C9E08E44093328126"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     an entity with respect to which a foreign person or combination of foreign persons described in subparagraph (A) directly or indirectly own at least a 20 percent stake; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H9D0B803211FE4B7EA0117E2C126BB6F5"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     a person subject to the direction or control of a foreign person or entity described in subparagraph (A) or (B).
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H15891EF7340F4CB1ADF6E2605DD37335"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  Data broker
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HBFB233DC49E446DABDB76A57037F94BA"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     In general
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">data broker means an entity that, for valuable consideration, sells, licenses, rents, trades, transfers, releases, discloses, provides access to, or otherwise makes available data of United States individuals that the entity did not collect directly from such individuals to another entity that is not acting as a service provider.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H6F61E075236849E1ABFB426BF22CD867"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Exclusion
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">data broker does not include an entity to the extent such entityâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H05EAF00997704758AAB75CB6B5FD5CCC"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        is transmitting data of a United States individual, including communications of such an individual, at the request or direction of such individual;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H671B42518A764814BF0F780ACACA8FB4"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        is providing, maintaining, or offering a product or service with respect to which personally identifiable sensitive data, or access to such data, is not the product or service;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H7770C5C80E754EAB89AB6E5EE66ED799"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iii)
                        is reporting or publishing news or information that concerns local, national, or international events or other matters of public interest;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H86CE68F6C6774729A133BD584F31717F"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iv)
                        is reporting, publishing, or otherwise making available news or information that is available to the general publicâ€”
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="H8985BE53D0394C8FAA195629B5295A67"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (I)
                           including information fromâ€”
                           <item display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                  id="H7677C99E44CE4102B966C6D411009BC6"
                                  qb-display-quote="yes">
                              (aa)
                              a book, magazine, telephone book, or online directory;
                           
                           <item display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                  id="HCBD0E55254CA4B4FB71C2AA28AC0058F"
                                  qb-display-quote="yes">
                              (bb)
                              a motion picture;
                           
                           <item display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                  id="H78014C47661946ACB913828C65A6AC3F"
                                  qb-display-quote="yes">
                              (cc)
                              a television, internet, or radio program;
                           
                           <item display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                  id="HAB8BF818ED9D41C888273FDFFEC8F4FF"
                                  qb-display-quote="yes">
                              (dd)
                              the news media; or
                           
                           <item display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                  id="H7F1B26ECF5224269BB38B3EBAC4A5819"
                                  qb-display-quote="yes">
                              (ee)
                              an internet site that is available to the general public on an unrestricted basis; and
                           
                        
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="HBC8E7DC49B9E49DB9DAEE813743671FD"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (II)
                           not including an obscene visual depiction (as such term is used in section 1460 of title 18, United States Code); or
                        
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H684623A31619448FB80FE52F205E5AB9"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (v)
                        is acting as a service provider.
                     
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB5A44FBE333A4AC48DA1BF1CDFC181E4"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (4)
                  Foreign adversary country
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">foreign adversary country means a country specified in section 4872(d)(2) of title 10, United States Code.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HE33A6D6E5102441F8A6DF531CACC017F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (5)
                  Personally identifiable sensitive data
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">personally identifiable sensitive data means any sensitive data that identifies or is linked or reasonably linkable, alone or in combination with other data, to an individual or a device that identifies or is linked or reasonably linkable to an individual.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H45A63AE3AB3F45DEB858EC5240E70623"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (6)
                  Precise geolocation information
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">precise geolocation information means information thatâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H2207F0B01E3444DB958599D731FE1AD1"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     is derived from a device or technology of an individual; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H63858C7C1BDA46638187BE474D66BE4B"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     reveals the past or present physical location of an individual or device that identifies or is linked or reasonably linkable to 1 or more individuals, with sufficient precision to identify street level location information of an individual or device or the location of an individual or device within a range of 1,850 feet or less.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA69ADAC1025748DD83ABBE9530DCC381"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (7)
                  Sensitive data
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">sensitive data includes the following:
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HFCCC87A3AEAD4044B359C6B287653692"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     A government-issued identifier, such as a Social Security number, passport number, or driverâ€™s license number.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H6DF03C4969114A8C8A2C4EAF8BE634B6"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Any information that describes or reveals the past, present, or future physical health, mental health, disability, diagnosis, or healthcare condition or treatment of an individual.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H2FE7997705024BFD80A6E78CF1D63C38"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     A financial account number, debit card number, credit card number, or information that describes or reveals the income level or bank account balances of an individual.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H5D579D22F55840AB97C5251D48724258"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (D)
                     Biometric information.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HA3270327A95E488DA5D4DFCDB6648080"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (E)
                     Genetic information.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H430387D7A9C44F148F6B708EA8FBC06E"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (F)
                     Precise geolocation information.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HDC16FBF428754271A42EAFF2D4C0EFB4"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (G)
                     An individualâ€™s private communications such as voicemails, emails, texts, direct messages, mail, voice communications, and video communications, or information identifying the parties to such communications or pertaining to the transmission of such communications, including telephone numbers called, telephone numbers from which calls were placed, the time calls were made, call duration, and location information of the parties to the call.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HD4E38D24BA2A4671B3FA50527A294BCB"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (H)
                     Account or device log-in credentials, or security or access codes for an account or device.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H47BEBE82CC884C89A2EAA50546646585"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (I)
                     Information identifying the sexual behavior of an individual.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H3AB97FEDA91D4B03A221A31AA47413EE"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (J)
                     Calendar information, address book information, phone or text logs, photos, audio recordings, or videos, maintained for private use by an individual, regardless of whether such information is stored on the individualâ€™s device or is accessible from that device and is backed up in a separate location.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HA8505A1960534F60BB28E623D76BCD6A"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (K)
                     A photograph, film, video recording, or other similar medium that shows the naked or undergarment-clad private area of an individual.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC00403B0F543454095348A3E0A061F42"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (L)
                     Information revealing the video content requested or selected by an individual. 
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H297176DBA80743ADB5D3CB118E4185E1"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (M)
                     Information about an individual under the age of 17.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H2D935116CD154F7CAD23BF6E09061BAF"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (N)
                     An individualâ€™s race, color, ethnicity, or religion.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HDF6D6018BBFB401F997B1FED2FBE9AEE"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (O)
                     Information identifying an individualâ€™s online activities over time and across websites or online services.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HD2F266C582E242919686AEAE69ED2401"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (P)
                     Information that reveals the status of an individual as a member of the Armed Forces.
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H0C5D521ACC7D41EA8A417C6BB6D2BF6F"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (Q)
                     Any other data that a data broker sells, licenses, rents, trades, transfers, releases, discloses, provides access to, or otherwise makes available to a foreign adversary country, or entity that is controlled by a foreign adversary, for the purpose of identifying the types of data listed in subparagraphs (A) through (P).
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB3A7CF047751492E85587431C5D3E1C3"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (8)
                  Service provider
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">service provider means an entity thatâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H7B3CEAF1D3B94F8FAF5DC7A3F55BF1FA"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     collects, processes, or transfers data on behalf of, and at the direction ofâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H2D94019B119241F281B1B199D7B44BF7"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        an individual or entity that is not a foreign adversary country or controlled by a foreign adversary; or
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H384385917C6E434A8F777C6FCB7EC547"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        a Federal, State, Tribal, territorial, or local government entity; and
                     
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H8C82312E48074A15BD4F16A675E8709F"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     receives data from or on behalf of an individual or entity described in subparagraph (A)(i) or a Federal, State, Tribal, territorial, or local government entity.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HCF92F451955D41C6B3115024578A1AD3"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (9)
                  United States individual
                  The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">United States individual means a natural person residing in the United States.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H47B9A02AB0454545A305F3DC2AC196EB"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               Effective date
               This section shall take effect on the date that is 60 days after the date of the enactment of this division.
            
         
      
      
         J
         SHIP Act 
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H355B0839D2504984AC8D0DDB816C80BD"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            1.
            SHORT TITLE
            This division may be cited as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">Stop Harboring Iranian Petroleum Act or the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">SHIP Act.
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H40ED88438B99478A867922A13E91BF85"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            2.
            STATEMENT OF POLICY
            It is the policy of the United Statesâ€”
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H815B662D5A324342A993ACCFED894825"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (1)
               to deny Iran the ability to engage in destabilizing activities, support international terrorism, fund the development and acquisition of weapons of mass destruction and the means to deliver such weapons by limiting export of petroleum and petroleum products by Iran; 
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HE0305FA9F5954B25B6019E69DE1836FB"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (2)
               to deny Iran funds to oppress and commit human rights violations against the Iranian people assembling to peacefully redress the Iranian regime;
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HEE51F08E284C41D99451C88354AF045F"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (3)
               to fully enforce sanctions against those entities which provide support to the Iranian energy sector; and
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HE47727672FD24D09B14C0B88A30F985D"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (4)
               to counter Iranâ€™s actions to finance and facilitate the participation of foreign terrorist organizations in ongoing conflicts and illicit activities due to the threat such actions pose to the vital national interests of the United States.
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H722ED26A5D364CC896242C7D330446BE"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            3.
            IMPOSITION OF SANCTIONS WITH RESPECT TO IRANIAN PETROLEUM
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H0F2A4209405E47408CEFB67343556B24"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               On and after the date that is 180 days after the date of the enactment of this division, and except as provided in subsection (e)(2), the President shall impose the sanctions described in subsection (c) with respect to each foreign person that the President determines knowingly engaged, on or after such date of enactment, in an activity described in subsection (b).
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H39C09355288E4BAA8F12F787AC3523E1"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Activities described
               A foreign person engages in an activity described in this subsection if the foreign personâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H9FAD52E145E84BC5B2EB021F6C24F066"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  owns or operates a foreign port at which, on or after the date of the enactment of this division, such person knowingly permits to dock a vesselâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H0F693424723D49EF99C6765BC8A44B7A"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     that is included on the list of specially designated nationals and blocked persons maintained by the Office of Foreign Assets Control of the Department of the Treasury for transporting Iranian crude oil or petroleum products; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H4A744C3411114850A12464413097F135"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
