            3.
            SEVERABILITY
            If any provision of this division, or the application of such provision to any person or circumstance, is found to be unconstitutional, the remainder of this division, or the application of that provision to other persons or circumstances, shall not be affected.
         
      
      
         M
         Hamas and Other Palestinian Terrorist Groups International Financing Prevention Act 
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H4E767407A4624E4FACF2121A826ADA37"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            1.
            SHORT TITLE
            This division may be cited as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">Hamas and Other Palestinian Terrorist Groups International Financing Prevention Act.
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H51CCFF63355242BABB3DC971AECA05D4"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            2.
            STATEMENT OF POLICY
            It shall be the policy of the United Statesâ€”
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HF5269FDE96B346C6B8ED8EDD4CFB3B2E"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (1)
               to prevent Hamas, Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof from accessing its international support networks; and
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H6137A6E02F884E1E99D0DB81A88CF600"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (2)
               to oppose Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof from using goods, including medicine and dual use items, to smuggle weapons and other materials to further acts of terrorism, including against Israel.
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H30EC501A32834286BCE46F1375ECD35B"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            3.
            IMPOSITION OF SANCTIONS WITH RESPECT TO FOREIGN PERSONS SUPPORTING ACTS OF TERRORISM OR ENGAGING IN SIGNIFICANT TRANSACTIONS WITH SENIOR MEMBERS OF HAMAS, PALESTINIAN ISLAMIC JIHAD AND OTHER PALESTINIAN TERRORIST ORGANIZATIONS
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H3B133C8251824FD3BA2F5FAEE6FB0D99"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               Not later than 180 days after the date of enactment of this division, the President shall impose the sanctions described in subsection (c) with respect to each foreign person that the President determines, on or after the date of the enactment of this division, engages in an activity described in subsection (b).
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H57AE15A3DD8D4AECB58BB75C6935799C"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Activities described
               A foreign person engages in an activity described in this subsection if the foreign person knowinglyâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H66C1F8E8BCFB4808964DCA83933081EB"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  assists in sponsoring or providing significant financial, material, or technological support for, or goods or other services to enable, acts of terrorism; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H48410D5BDDB04446A17C9618FC18DFA0"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  engages, directly or indirectly, in a significant transaction withâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HB6000C517B9F4CAE9017F70B1590A0DB"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     a senior member of Hamas, Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H7088568A17CA429BAE8D995FDF60711F"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     a senior member of a foreign terrorist organization designated pursuant to section 219 of the Immigration and Nationality Act (8 U.S.C. 1189) that is responsible for providing, directly or indirectly, support to Hamas, Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof.
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H79279EF21C36443D9928D2FD22A7E046"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Sanctions described
               The President shall exercise all of the powers granted to the President under the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1701 et seq.) to the extent necessary to block and prohibit all transactions in property and interests in property of a foreign person described in subsection (a) if such property and interests in property are in the United States, come within the United States, or are or come within the possession or control of a United States person.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HA869803DB9974C43ABEF49079E595FF2"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               Penalties
               The penalties provided for in subsections (b) and (c) of section 206 of the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1705) shall apply to a person that violates, attempts to violate, conspires to violate, or causes a violation of this section or any regulations promulgated to carry out this section to the same extent that such penalties apply to a person that commits an unlawful act described in section 206(a) of that Act.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HFFD6764F24264D888E136947D3BBB037"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (e)
               Implementation; regulations
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H3A5D6D408FEE4B3EA3CC9172A3FF4B13"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  The President may exercise all authorities provided under sections 203 and 205 of the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1702 and 1704) for purposes of carrying out this section.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD61579C963C942D082822D7FF4CE6380"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Regulations
                  Not later than 60 days after the date of the enactment of this division, the President shall issue regulations or other guidance as may be necessary for the implementation of this section.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HD65303FED37A4E2382F57546CDB5C2C1"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (f)
               Waiver
               The President may waive, on a case-by-case basis and for a period of not more than 180 days, the application of sanctions under this section with respect to a foreign person only if, not later than 15 days prior to the date on which the waiver is to take effect, the President submits to the appropriate congressional committees a written determination and justification that the waiver is in the vital national security interests of the United States.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H2A596A3CF9F0481D9A88C9A8DADF4E3F"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (g)
               Humanitarian assistance
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HEB646CEEEFD34C4CADC7EE1589B6E4A1"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  Sanctions under this section shall not apply toâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HD21D584D30E949F78472EEC1D670AE94"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     the conduct or facilitation of a transaction for the provision of agricultural commodities, food, medicine, medical devices, or humanitarian assistance, or for humanitarian purposes; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HF473CF0D67124DF5BD7D82CFF59CE272"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     transactions that are necessary for or related to the activities described in subparagraph (A).
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H102AEFA11C8343E39122383F5A295C53"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Definitions
                  In this subsection:
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H6895278F9A6346C59DB7C3A0C929D22E"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     Agricultural commodity
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">agricultural commodity has the meaning given that term in section 102 of the Agricultural Trade Act of 1978 (7 U.S.C. 5602).
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H8905FC74A9F94042B0D03D7EA4298E9C"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Medical device
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">medical device has the meaning given the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">device in section 201 of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (21 U.S.C. 321).
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H31A4BFBE73334663A6AB6994EF9A1384"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     Medicine
                     The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">medicine has the meaning given the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                quote-display-start="auto"
                                quote-type="text">drug in section 201 of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (21 U.S.C. 321).
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H3CBD53BEFF0C47FD96105257B943FAA7"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (h)
               Rule of construction
               The authority to impose sanctions under this section with respect to a foreign person is in addition to the authority to impose sanctions under any other provision of law with respect to a foreign person that directly or indirectly supports acts of international terrorism.
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H7709630B69E24728AB50A7CC1263EE6E"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            4.
            IMPOSITION OF MEASURES WITH RESPECT TO FOREIGN STATES PROVIDING SUPPORT TO HAMAS, PALESTINIAN ISLAMIC JIHAD AND OTHER PALESTINIAN TERRORIST ORGANIZATIONS
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H86FD52518F3C4C11899B1191170D4645"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               Not later than 180 days after the date of enactment of this division, the President shall impose the measures described in subsection (c) with respect to a foreign state if the President determines that the foreign state, on or after the date of the enactment of this division, engages in an activity described in subsection (b).
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H5700AE60D9FE4DD19EE608B795E109FA"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Activities described
               A foreign state engages in an activity described in this subsection if the foreign state knowinglyâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H46325685E52E46A5A5E8B46E5FAB6D9F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  provides significant material or financial support for acts of international terrorism, pursuant toâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HBBAB00ABD6724FD1803335BBF996704F"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     section 1754(c) of the Export Control Reform Act of 2018 (50 U.S.C. 4813(c)(1)(A));
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HAB6D242099604FEEB8F3D490F75D3D82"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     section 620A of the Foreign Assistance Act of 1961 (22 U.S.C. 2371);
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HE4D050E9A7E843A08F120B4538177CC6"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (C)
                     section 40 of the Arms Export Control Act (22 U.S.C. 2780); or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HCD6B2AB60FD24E9F9830A26E68C89D96"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (D)
                     any other provision of law;
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB29C7D5CA48342E18F06488EA688D019"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  provides significant material support to Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HFB1450CB43B04654A11F49F7472156B0"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  engages in a significant transaction that materially contributes, directly or indirectly, to the terrorist activities of Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HC19316D94DB34A4F8F5C7343B1C271FC"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Measures described
               The measures described in this subsection with respect to a foreign state are the following:
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HF3A9ADA9DB8C4BC8A020B2DC9EA6DD20"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  The President shall suspend, for a period of at least 1 year, United States assistance to the foreign state.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H5E5B99F8CF334DB2A126B5E2AA688982"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  The Secretary of the Treasury shall instruct the United States Executive Director to each appropriate international financial institution to oppose, and vote against, for a period of 1 year, the extension by such institution of any loan or financial or technical assistance to the government of the foreign state.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H45C3F415AAB44CE1AD9C39747FA814ED"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  The President shall prohibit the export of any item on the United States Munitions List (established pursuant to section 38 of the Arms Export Control Act (22 U.S.C. 2778)) or the Commerce Control List set forth in Supplement No. 1 to part 774 of title 15, Code of Federal Regulations, to the foreign state for a period of 1 year.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H89E9E2EDB8F545DEAC06D23BFA3FA34D"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               Penalties
               The penalties provided for in subsections (b) and (c) of section 206 of the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1705) shall apply to a person that violates, attempts to violate, conspires to violate, or causes a violation of this section or any regulations promulgated to carry out this section to the same extent that such penalties apply to a person that commits an unlawful act described in section 206(a) of that Act.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H81E87F44131840C39D5062BDB3ED628B"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (e)
               Waiver
               The President may waive, on a case-by-case basis and for a period of not more than 180 days, the application of measures under this section with respect to a foreign state only if, not later than 15 days prior to the date on which the waiver is to take effect, the President submits to the appropriate congressional committees a written determination and justification that the waiver is in the vital national security interests of the United States.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H3C21BDC024CD48638A9F53AFA1CD9C10"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (f)
               Implementation; regulations
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H09977A6F8E04407CB1E2E063D0B5760B"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  The President may exercise all authorities provided under sections 203 and 205 of the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1702 and 1704) for purposes of carrying out this section.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H2870AF5121F14F16B558CA4EAF8576BC"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Regulations
                  Not later than 60 days after the date of the enactment of this division, the President shall issue regulations or other guidance as may be necessary for the implementation of this section.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H669988338BBB43FE95C68284EDE84BEA"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (g)
               Additional exemptions
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H9D137BA233CB42D48B684912FB853000"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Status of forces agreements
                  The President may exempt the application of measures under this section with respect to a foreign state if the application of such measures would prevent the United States from meeting the terms of any status of forces agreement to which the United States is a party or meeting other obligations relating to the basing of United States service members.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HBDA4DC37128C44E6982904C4A13FF9D1"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">

                  Authorized intelligence activities

               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H16D52BB5A2DE4581A3634AC14921DE52"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  Humanitarian assistance
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H580B8B5EB44C4CC8BD852808E0B20256"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     In general
                     Measures under this section shall not apply toâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H2439C74561C843898A1E39DE165E26C8"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        the conduct or facilitation of a transaction for the provision of agricultural commodities, food, medicine, medical devices, or humanitarian assistance, or for humanitarian purposes; or
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H07A293218E2443B2933E908FACE7EBAC"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        transactions that are necessary for or related to the activities described in clause (i).
                     
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HC4306CC88D94454F921DA5B166003F0A"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     Definitions
                     In this subsection:
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HFB035A42A698453F8D3AA970A7CFCBB8"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        Agricultural commodity
                        The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                   quote-display-start="auto"
                                   quote-type="text">agricultural commodity has the meaning given that term in section 102 of the Agricultural Trade Act of 1978 (7 U.S.C. 5602).
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HED83958400734417A32362F3B014B94F"

                        Medical device
                        The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                   quote-display-start="auto"
                                   quote-type="text">medical device has the meaning given the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                   quote-display-start="auto"
                                   quote-type="text">device in section 201 of the Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (21 U.S.C. 321).
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HCFEADF5B4EA24B4A921935C96A28CAEF"

                        Medicine
                        The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                   quote-display-start="auto"
                                   quote-type="text">medicine has the meaning given the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                                   quote-display-start="auto"

            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"

            5.
            REPORTS ON ACTIVITIES TO DISRUPT GLOBAL FUNDRAISING, FINANCING, AND MONEY LAUNDERING ACTIVITIES OF HAMAS, PALESTINIAN ISLAMIC JIHAD, AL-AQSA MARTYRS BRIGADE, THE LIONâ€™S DEN OR ANY AFFILIATE OR SUCCESSOR THEREOF
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H0479DEA9B8B54CFD9EE3E6ED5CACC3EF"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               Not later than 90 days after the date of enactment of this division, and every 180 days thereafter, the President shall submit to the appropriate congressional committees a report that includesâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA9F0EC316A224D4BB0BEDB34D3066A03"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  an assessment of the disposition of the assets and activities of Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof related to fundraising, financing, and money laundering worldwide;
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H6DAC9D53A63C4C76A5995D8AE42D4ED8"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  a list of foreign states that knowingly providing material, financial, or technical support for, or goods or services to Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof;
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H9E0B8C6E7FDC409DBEF9F8B25690EAB9"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  a list of foreign states in which Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof conducts significant fundraising, financing, or money laundering activities;
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HEF3C1249C9114D659E72EF1E76363ADB"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (4)
                  a list of foreign states from which Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliate or successor thereof knowingly engaged in the transfer of surveillance equipment, electronic monitoring equipment, or other means to inhibit communication or the free flow of information in Gaza; and
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB68AC219A0DE48D5BA5BAA53279C6D97"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (5)
                  with respect to each foreign state listed in paragraph (2), (3), or (4)â€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HECF1FABEE12442C9B7AC0228334F70F5"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     a description of the steps the foreign state identified is taking adequate measures to restrict financial flows to Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, or any affiliates or successors thereof; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H178EAC40FAC74C99A80C86AD6BF11EFC"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     in the case of a foreign state failing to take adequate measures to restrict financial flows to Hamas, Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den or any other designated entity engaged in significant act of terrorism threatening the peace and security of Israelâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H7E17A0A02BA8409EA8D665FDDFBEEB97"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        an assessment of the reasons that government is not taking adequate measures to restrict financial flows to those entities; and
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HD9DAB13B13174FA195592EC241C19871"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        a description of measures being taken by the United States Government to encourage the foreign state to restrict financial flows to those entities; and
                     
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"

                         qb-display-quote="yes">

               Form

            6.
            TERMINATION
            This division shall terminate on the earlier ofâ€”
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HD9E8534F652C433481EC25709BE3EC88"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (1)
               the date that is 7 years after the date of the enactment of this division; or
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H3B9219806F9E417E9559597672EA1C38"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (2)
               the date that is 30 days after the date on which the President certifies to the appropriate congressional committees thatâ€”
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HFDFCE4152A3F4D28ABD68D23B7409AB0"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (A)
                  Hamas or any successor or affiliate thereof is no longer designated as a foreign terrorist organization pursuant to section 219 of the Immigration and Nationality Act (8 U.S.C. 1189);
               
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H95AAB9B1DADA413BB79C4B23B03AAA02"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (B)
                  Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, and any successor or affiliate thereof are no longer subject to sanctions pursuant toâ€”
                  <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H261B643B9E094E74B91B5A9B3D98E319"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (i)
                     Executive Order No. 12947 (January 23, 1995; relating to prohibiting transactions with terrorists who threaten to disrupt the Middle East peace process); and
                  
                  <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HF5342249E2B6478DBCB7E1F02CF17745"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (ii)
                     Executive Order No. 13224 (September 23, 2001; relating to blocking property and prohibiting transactions with persons who commit, threaten to commit, or support terrorism); and
                  
               
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HBA7D910158CB416E9BC9C57540F39CB0"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (C)
                  Hamas, the Palestinian Islamic Jihad, Al-Aqsa Martyrs Brigade, the Lionâ€™s Den, and any successor or affiliate thereof meet the criteria described in paragraphs (1) through (4) of section 9 of the Palestinian Anti-Terrorism Act of 2006 (22 U.S.C. 2378b note).
               
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H31104B55EDC44B39A6550518330CA013"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            7.
            DEFINITIONS
            In this division:
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HB5D84E6B409F4926B82A1973F893606B"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (1)
               Act of terrorism
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">act of terrorism means an activity thatâ€”
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H95479CFDBE6E4D318EC48F39DB16FBE1"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (A)
                  involves a violent act or an act dangerous to human life, property, or infrastructure; and
               
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HF3AB11EE8AD94D6C9633D293BD7859F3"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (B)
                  appears to be intended toâ€”
                  <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H11EA8D5E4DAF40F5BB428244339E36A6"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (i)
                     intimidate or coerce a civilian population;
                  
                  <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB6891E36208447FA8057A7F90AA4CD01"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (ii)
                     influence the policy of a government by intimidation or coercion; or
                  
                  <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD0AA04E46C3541C59888123C468C8F9A"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (iii)
                     affect the conduct of a government by mass destruction, assassination, kidnapping, or hostage-taking.
                  
               
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H2CAB0DE214A142ACB1954BE7632D75A9"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (2)
               Admitted
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">admitted has the meaning given such term in section 101(a)(13)(A) of the Immigration and Nationality Act (8 U.S.C. 1101(a)(13)(A)).
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H1A0AF6448B7B4739AD144E91516A6345"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (3)
               Appropriate congressional committees
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">appropriate congressional committees meansâ€”
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H675386C76DD948C1A5022D9644D15923"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (A)
                  the Committee on Foreign Affairs and the Committee on Financial Services of the House of Representatives; and
               
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H1577F63C33584E4FB80D6B79429B3FF4"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (B)
                  the Committee on Foreign Relations and the Committee on Banking, Housing, and Urban Affairs of the Senate.
               
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="HB1513C2A32124F50A86BC021943AF71A"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (4)
               Foreign state
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">foreign state has the meaning given such term in section 1603 of title 28, United States Code.
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H1EFFB691BD6C4AA9821CE7420C3F28BB"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (5)
               Humanitarian aid
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">humanitarian aid means food, medicine, and medical supplies.
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H9C9CBA02A1AE449CA8B425DDD1CD8DEF"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (6)
               Material support
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">material support has the meaning given the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">material support or resources in section 2339A of title 18, United States Code.
            
            <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                        id="H3C041807ADE342F7838BC674016D78A4"
                        qb-display-quote="yes">
               (7)
               United states person
               The term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">United States person meansâ€”
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H1D07685021DD441AA8F5F4DF6327DDCA"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (A)
                  a United States citizen or an alien lawfully admitted for permanent residence to the United States; or
               
               <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H94F201D5C84E47F6932CDF7139DB72C8"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">

                  an entity organized under the laws of the United States or of any jurisdiction within the United States, including a foreign branch of such an entity.
               
            
         
      
      
         N
         No Technology for Terror Act 
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H543BEFE170D94ED58D8685F1F7BB0F9D"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            1.
            SHORT TITLE
            This division may be cited as the <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                       quote-display-start="auto"
                       quote-type="text">
                  No Technology for Terror Act
               . 
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="HE98AC784FB1B4A0481FF49D68BD4629B"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            2.
            APPLICATION OF FOREIGN-DIRECT PRODUCT RULES TO IRAN
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HD7BA7DCE023B4E79B1336D8168566FC0"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               Beginning on the date that is 90 days after the date of the enactment of this division, a foreign-produced item shall be subject to the Export Administration Regulations (pursuant to the Export Control Reform Act of 2018 (50 U.S.C. 4801 et seq.)) if the itemâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA84AADBDA6B64E43B7EF72A41A579038"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  meetsâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H6707A05244B14720910073DC55DDE9BD"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     the product scope requirements described in subsection (b); and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HCA6CC324CCA54374BF34ADD428081128"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     the destination scope requirements described in subsection (c); and
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H08A7D9D0C5854652A247D1CE9777CE7A"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  is exported, reexported, or in-country transferred to Iran from abroad or involves the Government of Iran.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H1497F19BEBBB45669A5B955023C3AA43"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Product scope requirements
               A foreign-produced item meets the product scope requirements of this subsection if the itemâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H7FE5DBB95349420FA7AC36061223B34F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  is a direct product of United States-origin technology or software subject to the Export Administration Regulations that is specified in a covered Export Control Classification Number or is identified in supplement no. 7 to part 746 of the Export Administration Regulations; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H18A900552E4E459495EE5F3BAE7238B5"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  is produced by any plant or major component of a plant that is located outside the United States, if the plant or major component of a plant, whether made in the United States or a foreign country, itself is a direct product of United States-origin technology or software subject to the Export Administration Regulations that is specified in a covered Export Control Classification Number.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H688737B7208E4DEE8344B1DF7ACC379D"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Destination scope requirements
               A foreign-produced item meets the destination scope requirements of this subsection if there is knowledge that the foreign-produced item is destined to Iran or will be incorporated into or used in the production or development of any part, component, or equipment subject to the Export Administration Regulations and produced in or destined to Iran.
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H116FA969922C41BD8074F071817FC184"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               License requirements
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H8DB3C7F82C6C4F5D9DD960A9FCE4511B"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  A license shall be required to export, reexport, or in-country transfer a foreign-produced item from abroad that meets the product scope requirements described in subsection (b) and the destination scope requirements described in subsection (c) and is subject to the Export Administration Regulations pursuant to this section.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H6944576C42004E2BB4BE947AF5A68C0C"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Exceptions
                  The license requirements of paragraph (1) shall not apply toâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H67E50B9FC1974D839EB04380AAFC57AE"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     food, medicine, or medical devices that areâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HD61BC31354B348D3BA96F245031F842E"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        designated as EAR99; or
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H29E31984FC4A4714B29DDDEA37390345"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        not designated under or listed on the Commerce Control List; or
                     
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H7C917BEA730C4783B1B34A9195D53B06"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     services, software, or hardware (other than services, software, or hardware for end-users owned or controlled by the Government of Iran) that areâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HCFBC10EFF0184A76A0ED6035F20FD94C"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        necessarily and ordinarily incident to communications; or
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H6A905EBE81E14BAE8E7B109070372F48"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        designated asâ€”
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="H129D30FF52EB477BBF5B388A69F6735E"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (I)
                           EAR99; or
                        
                        <subclause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                    id="H894A657252CF40B7AB950DBD2D03F0E7"
                                    qb-display-quote="yes">
                           (II)
                           Export Control Classification Number 5A992.c or 5D992.c, and classified in accordance with section 740.17 of title 15 Code of Federal Regulations; and
                        
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H69A7E6AD7DEC40DCA688EEB1E7131EEA"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iii)
                        subject to a general license issued by the Department of Commerce or Department of Treasury.
                     
                  
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H6C3C859B6D8F4AD89F8DB823A48EDA8E"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (e)
               National interest waiver
               The Secretary of Commerce may waive the requirements imposed under this section if the Secretaryâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB897A9ACB1E44A22AC79187A2F199EEC"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  determines that the waiver is in the national interests of the United States; and
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HD8A59324E69C4166AA99D836A47A7D9D"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  submits to the Committee on Foreign Affairs and the Committee on Financial Services of the House of Representatives and to the Committee on Foreign Relations and the Committee on Banking, Housing, and Urban Affairs of the Senate a report explaining which requirements are being waived and the reasons for the waiver.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H750D605CF65743BBBA7DB77EC314C4C1"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (f)
               Sunset
               The authority provided under this section shall terminate on the date that is 7 years after the date of the enactment of this division.

               Definitions
               In this sectionâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"

                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">Commerce Control List means the list maintained pursuant to part 744 of the Export Administration Regulations;

               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"

                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  the terms <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"
                             quote-type="text">Export Administration Regulations, <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                             quote-display-start="auto"

               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"

            STATEMENT OF POLICY
            It shall be the policy of the United States to fully implement and enforce sanctions against terrorist organizations and other malign actors that use innocent civilians as human shields.

                     6.
                     SEVERABILITY
                     If any provision of this Act, or the application of such provision to any person or circumstance, is found to be unconstitutional, the remainder of this Act, or the application of that provision to other persons or circumstances, shall not be affected.

         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="HFC6A4C34302E434D9AA5CF00D33E5C01"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            4.
            REPORT ON COUNTERING THE USE OF HUMAN SHIELDS
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HC71C671A9DB040E7A1A25B0775F9D193"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               Not later than 120 days after the date of the enactment of this division, the Secretary of Defense shall submit to the congressional defense committees, the Committee on Foreign Affairs of the House of Representatives, and the Committee on Foreign Relations of the Senate a report that contains the following:
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H9F816F78385240C196F87F31CDAFCD50"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  A description of the lessons learned from the United States and its allies and partners in addressing the use of human shields by terrorist organizations such as Hamas, Hezbollah, Palestine Islamic Jihad, and any other organization as determined by the Secretary of Defense.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HB0A8E3E8541A4E41915FF78006A857F2"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  A description of a specific plan and actions being taken by the Department of Defense to incorporate the lessons learned as identified in paragraph (1) into Department of Defense operating guidance, relevant capabilities, and tactics, techniques, and procedures to deter, counter, and address the challenge posed by the use of human shields and hold accountable terrorist organizations for the use of human shields.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HACE48B1455864DE4ADB1C90213A3F4F1"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  A description of specific measures being developed and implemented by the United States Government to mobilize and leverage allied nations, including member nations of the North Atlantic Treaty Organization (NATO), to deter, counter, and hold accountable terrorist organizations for the use of human shields.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H9F23C9CDD3E84559BAE0CFB6E39BADD9"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (4)
                  The current status of joint exercises, doctrine development, education, and training on countering the use of human shields in multinational centers of excellence.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA6A1990668534AADAB1D410572E0146D"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (5)
                  The current status of participation of members of the Armed Forces and Department of Defense civilian personnel in any multinational center of excellence for the purposes of countering the use of human shields.
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H6011B95863FC4D8CBCBFA660C6551150"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (6)
                  The feasibility and advisability of beginning or continuing participation of members of the Armed Forces and Department of Defense civilian personnel to promote the integration of joint exercises, doctrine development, education, and training on countering the use of human shields into multinational centers of excellence.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="HD9CA14BC03EB43C5A85BA79F613D3DDC"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Definition
               In this section, the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">multinational center of excellence has the meaning given that term in section 344 of title 10, United States Code.
            
         
         <section display-inline="no-display-inline"
                   id="H98E6028FF28D4F0DAE5E9FF20B3117D3"
                   qb-display-quote="yes"
                   section-type="subsequent-section">
            5.
            CONFRONTING ASYMMETRIC AND MALICIOUS CYBER ACTIVITIES
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H244D4E754A6E4018833FD1685941A221"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (a)
               In general
               On and after the date that is 180 days after the date of the enactment of this division, the President may impose the sanctions described in subsection (b) with respect to any foreign person that the Secretary of the Treasury, in consultation with the Attorney General and the Secretary of State determine, on or after such date of enactmentâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H55A442D5D9D047BB874F65BEA3A1B72A"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  is responsible for or complicit in, or has engaged knowingly in, significant cyber-enabled activities originating from, or directed by persons located, in whole or in substantial part, outside the United States that are reasonably likely to result in, or have materially contributed to, a significant threat to the national security, foreign policy, or economic health or financial stability of the United States;
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H2A4A7B9C880348B89C371DB0B9AD6CD1"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  materially assisted, sponsored, or provided financial, material, or technological support for, or goods or services to or in support of, any activity described in this subsection or any person whose property and interests in property are blocked pursuant to this section;
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA60C9308E94B41368686BEF2E9989972"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (3)
                  is owned or controlled by, or has acted or purported to act for or on behalf of, directly or indirectly, any person whose property and interests in property are blocked pursuant to this section; or
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HC0FA8693EE7044789CBB8D1D67DD62D1"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (4)
                  has attempted to engage in any of the activities described in paragraph (1), (2), or (3).
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H4F5BE73150D4489CB94AC67EB15C7392"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (b)
               Sanctions described
               The sanctions described in this subsection are the following:
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H48752469B43D4A58B2C431F3E8BD8E8F"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  Inadmissibility to united states
                  In the case of an alienâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="HDFF4CFA7CBD64B5F906501635D8BA07C"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     ineligibility to receive a visa to enter the United States or to be admitted to the United States; or
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H7881A67CD19B4C6A8C013AF9157BEBFE"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     if the individual has been issued a visa or other documentation, revocation, in accordance with section 221(i) of the Immigration and Nationality Act (8 U.S.C. 1201(i)), of the visa or other documentation.
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HA3984B8422B04B02950497D234D54449"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Blocking of property
                  The blocking, in accordance with the International Emergency Economic Powers Act (50 U.S.C. 1701 et seq.), of all transactions in all property and interests in property of a foreign person if such property and interests in property are in the United States, come within the United States, or are or come within the possession or control of a United States person.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H43ECF749D0C54E319F49ADE8BD82E51F"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (c)
               Requests by appropriate congressional committees
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H4D94DCC7BCA54039BC080B90A19C1A1C"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (1)
                  In general
                  Not later than 120 days after receiving a request that meets the requirements of paragraph (2) with respect to whether a foreign person has engaged in an activity described in subsection (a), the Secretary of the Treasury, in consultation with the Attorney General and the Secretary of State shallâ€”
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H1D1E93DED7EA4541BA8EC7EBDDC1FB2B"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (A)
                     determine if that person has engaged in such an activity; and
                  
                  <subparagraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                                 id="H0A3F8C69C8224CCB8AA295EFF605EF8C"
                                 qb-display-quote="yes">
                     (B)
                     submit a classified or unclassified report to the chairperson and ranking member of the committee or committees that submitted the request with respect to that determination that includesâ€”
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H2BF50DD0F31D4E279B23746C871A0501"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (i)
                        a statement of whether or not the Secretary of the Treasury, in consultation with the Attorney General and the Secretary of State imposed or intends to impose sanctions with respect to the person;
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="HA6D04B75417E4094B8E94B836EA36760"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (ii)
                        if the President imposed or intends to impose sanctions, a description of those sanctions; and
                     
                     <clause display-inline="no-display-inline"
                              id="H9798FED515DB469D8A2CE18AA1961409"
                              qb-display-quote="yes">
                        (iii)
                        if the President does not intend to impose sanctions, a description of actions that meet the threshold for the President to impose sanctions.
                     
                  
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="HE51850D7E1DF4D0E8C914E19A342E1B6"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">
                  (2)
                  Requirements
                  A request under paragraph (1) with respect to whether a foreign person has engaged in an activity described in subsection (a) shall be submitted to the President in writing jointly by the chairperson and ranking member of one of the appropriate congressional committees.
               
            
            <subsection display-inline="no-display-inline"
                         id="H2870A813160F40BF8C5C4C960A0DBBBC"
                         qb-display-quote="yes">
               (d)
               Appropriate congressional committees defined
               In this section, the term <quote quote-display-end="auto"
                          quote-display-start="auto"
                          quote-type="text">appropriate congressional committees meansâ€”
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
                           id="H50A415EB62234B3982D5799260B3D000"
                           qb-display-quote="yes">

                  the Committee on Foreign Affairs, the Committee on Financial Services, and the Committee on the Judiciary of the House of Representatives; and
               
               <paragraph display-inline="no-display-inline"
